we could make a very long list , but obviously nelson mandela , emerging from 17 years of hard physical labor , 23 years of imprisonment , with this amazing ability to forgive , so that he could lead his nation out the evil regime of apartheid without a bloodbath .	我們可以列出很長的清單 , 但很顯然 , 曼德拉從17年的艱難實體勞動中湧現 , 23年的監禁性 , 讓他可以帶領他的國家 , 讓他沒有血腥的邪惡政權 。
ken sarowiwa , in nigeria , who took on the giant oil companies , and although people around the world tried their best , was executed .	kensarowiwa , 在奈及利亞 , 他採用了巨型石油公司 , 雖然全世界的人都盡了最好的努力 , 被執行 。
people like this are so inspirational .	像這樣的人是如此的鼓舞人心 。
people like this are the role models we need for young africans .	像這樣的人是年輕非洲人所需要的榜樣 。
and we need some environmental role models as well , and i've been hearing some of them today .	我們也需要一些環保的榜樣 , 今天我也聽到了其中一些 。
so i'm really grateful for this opportunity to share this message again , with everyone at ted .	所以 , 我真的很感激這個機會能再次分享這個訊息 , 和ted的所有人分享 。
and i hope that some of us can get together and talk about some of these things , especially the roots and shoots program .	我希望我們當中有些人可以聚在一起 , 談論這些事 , 特別是根和芽計畫 。
and just a last word on that the young woman who's running this entire conference center , i met her today .	最後一個詞語是 , 經營這整個會議中心的年輕女子 , 我今天見到她 。
she came up so excited , with her certificate . she was [in] roots and shoots .	她很興奮 , 用她的證據 , 她是根和芽 。
she was in the leadership in dar es salaam .	她在達爾•薩拉姆的領導力 。
she said it's helped her to do what she's doing .	她說 , 是幫助她做她正在做的事 。
and it was very , very exciting for me to meet her and see just one example of how young people , when they are empowered , given the opportunity to take action , to make the world a better place , truly are our hope for tomorrow .	對我來說 , 很興奮 , 讓我很興奮 , 看看年輕人如何被賦予力量 , 給予機會 , 讓世界變得更美好 , 真正是我們明天的希望 。
artist dianna cohen shares some tough truths about plastic pollution in the ocean and in our lives and some thoughts on how to free ourselves from the plastic gyre .	藝術家dannacohen分享了一些艱難的事實 , 關於塑膠污染的真相 , 以及我們生活中的一些思想 , 如何將我們自己從塑膠體中解放出來 。
consumerism , global issues , green , mission blue , oceans , plastic	消費主義、全球議題、綠色、使命藍色、海洋、塑膠、塑膠 。
dianna cohen: tough truths about plastic pollution	黛安娜.庫恩:關於塑膠污染的艱難真理:關於塑膠污染的艱難真理 。
i'm a visual artist , and i'm also one of the cofounders of the plastic pollution coalition .	我是一個視覺藝術家 , 我也是塑膠污染聯盟的共同創辦人之一 。
i've been working with plastic bags , which i cut up and sew back together as my primary material for my artwork for the last 20 years .	我一直在用塑膠袋 , 把塑膠袋切開 , 把它們縫在一起 , 用在我過去二十年的藝術作品中 。
i turn them into two and threedimensional pieces and sculptures and installations .	我把它們變成兩個三維的碎片、雕塑和裝置 。
upon working with the plastic , after about the first eight years , some of my work started to fissure and break down into smaller little bits of plastic .	和塑膠一起工作 , 大約十八年後 , 我的一些作品開始融化 , 分解成小小的塑膠 。
and i thought , " great .	我心想: 「 太棒了 。
it's ephemeral just like us . "	和我們一樣是多元的 。 」
upon educating myself a little further about plastics , i actually realized this was a bad thing .	教育我自己更進一步教育塑膠 , 我發現這是一件壞事 。
it's a bad thing that plastic breaks down into smaller little bits , because it's always still plastic .	塑膠會把塑膠分成小一點點 , 因為它一直都是塑膠 。
and what we're finding is that a lot of it is in the marine environment .	我們所發現的是 , 很多在海洋環境中 。
i then , in the last few years , learned about the pacific garbage patch and the gyre .	然後 , 在過去幾年 , 我學到了太平洋垃圾堆和蓋爾 。
and my initial reaction and i think this is a lot of people's first reaction to learning about it is , " oh my god !	而我最初的反應 , 我認為這是很多人最早的反應 , 就是 「 天啊 !
we've got to go out there and clean this thing up . "	我們必須去那裡清理這個東西 。 」
so i actually developed a proposal to go out with a cargo ship and two decommissioned fishing trawlers , a crane , a chipping machine and a coldmolding machine .	所以 , 我真的開發了一個提案 , 用一艘貨船和兩艘被驅逐的捕魚拖網 , 一台拖車 , 一台拖車 , 一台冷卻的機器 。
and my intention was to go out to the gyre , raise awareness about this issue and begin to pick up the plastic , chip it into little bits and cold mold it into bricks that could potentially be used as building materials in underdeveloped communities .	我的意圖是去到健身房 , 開始意識到這個議題 , 開始將塑膠切片切成碎片 , 冷卻的磚塊 , 可以用來當作隱藏社區的材料 。
i began talking with people who actually had been out to the gyre and were studying the plastic problem in the marine environment and upon doing so , i realized actually that cleaning it up would be a very small drop in the bucket relative to how much is being generated every day around the world , and that actually i needed to back up and look at the bigger picture .	我開始和那些真的去過健身和研究海洋環境中的塑膠問題談話 , 等等 , 我意識到 , 清理這些東西會是非常小的一滴 , 和全世界每天所產生的物質有多大 , 我真的需要回到過去 , 看看更大的照片 。
and the bigger picture is: we need to find a way to turn off the faucet .	更大的圖片是:我們需要找到一個方法來關閉水面 。
we need to cut the spigot of singleuse and disposable plastics , which are entering the marine environment every day on a global scale .	我們需要把單一use和不可取代塑膠的位置切割在全球各地的環境中 。
so in looking at that , i also realized that i was really angry .	仔細看 , 我也了解到 , 我真的很生氣 。
i wasn't just concerned about plastic that you're trying to imagine out in the middle of the pacific ocean of which i have learned there are now 11 gyres , potentially , of plastic in five major oceans in the world .	我不只關心塑膠 , 你在太平洋中間的想像 , 我學到現在有11個冰河 , 可能是世界上五個主要的海洋 。
it's not just that gyre of plastic that i'm concerned about it's the gyre of plastic in the supermarket .	不單只是我擔心的塑膠小屋 , 是超級市場的塑膠小屋 。
i'd go to the supermarket and all of my food is packaged in plastic .	我會去超市 , 所有的食物都包含在塑膠上 。
all of my beverages are packaged in plastic , even at the health food market .	我的所有平均都是塑膠包裝 , 甚至是健康食物市場 。
i'm also concerned about the plastic in the refrigerator , and i'm concerned about the plastic and the toxins that leach from plastic into us and into our bodies .	我也關心冰箱裡的塑膠 , 我關心塑膠和從塑膠帶到我們體內的毒素 。
so i came together with a group of other people who were all looking at this issue , and we created the plastic pollution coalition .	所以我和一群人一起研究這個議題 , 我們創造了塑膠污染聯盟 。
we have many initiatives that we're working on , but some of them are very basic .	我們有許多計畫 , 我們正在努力 , 但有些是非常基本的 。
one is: if 80 to 90 percent of what we're finding in the ocean of the marine debris that we're finding in the ocean is plastic , then why don't we call it what it is .	一是:如果我們在海洋中發現的生物有百分之八十到九十--我們在海洋中發現的生物是塑膠 , 那為什麼我們不把它稱之為它是什麼 。
recycling everybody kind of ends their books about being sustainable and greening with the idea of recycling .	回收所有人的書 , 都是關於永續和綠化 , 關於回收的概念 。
you put something in a bin and you don't have to think about it again .	你把某樣東西放進一個桶子裡 , 你不用再想一想 。
what is the reality of that ?	這是什麼樣的現實呢 ?
in the united states , less than seven percent of our plastics are recycled .	在美國 , 不到7%的塑膠回收 。
and if you really look into it , particularly when it comes to plastic bottles , most of it is only downcycled , or incinerated , or shipped to china .	如果你真的仔細觀察 , 尤其是當到塑膠瓶時 , 大部分的瓶子只會被回收 , 或被送到中國 。
it is downcycled and turned into lesser things , while a glass bottle can be a glass bottle again or can be used again a plastic bottle can never be a plastic bottle again .	它被降低 , 變成更少的東西 , 而玻璃瓶可以再次成為玻璃瓶 , 或是可以再次使用塑膠瓶 , 永遠不會是塑膠瓶 。
so this is a big issue for us .	這對我們來說是個大問題 。
another thing that we're looking at and asking people to think about is we've added a fourth r onto the front of the " reduce , reuse , recycle , " three r's , and that is refuse .	我們看到的另一件事是 , 請大家思考一下 , 我們在 「 減少、再利用、回收 」 前面加了第四個節目 , 拒絕了 。
whenever possible , refuse singleuse and disposable plastics .	不論如何 , 都拒絕單一和可取的塑膠 。
alternatives exist ; some of them are very oldschool .	替代方案存在 , 有些是很古老的學者 。
i myself am now collecting these cool pyrex containers and using those instead of glad and tupperware containers to store food in .	我現在正在收集這些很酷的pyrex容器 , 用這些裝置 , 而不是放鬆和提醒容器來儲存食物 。
and i know that i am doing a service to myself and my family .	我知道我在為自己和家人做一個服務 。
it's very easy to pick up a stainlesssteel bottle or a glass bottle , if you're traveling and you've forgotten to bring your stainlesssteel bottle and fill that up with water or filtered water , versus purchasing plastic bottled water .	很容易就能拿起一瓶無菌的瓶子或玻璃瓶 , 如果你在旅行 , 你就忘了把你的不穩定的瓶子裝滿水或過濾過濾的水 , 對抗塑膠瓶瓶水 。
i guess what i want to say to everybody here and i know that you guys know a lot about this issue is that this is a huge problem in the oceans , but this is a problem that we've created as consumers and we can solve .	我猜我想跟大家說的 , 我知道你們都知道這個議題 , 就是這在海洋中是個很大的問題 , 但這是我們作為消費者所創造的一個問題 , 我們可以解決這個問題 。
we can solve this by raising awareness of the issue and teaching people to choose alternatives .	我們可以藉由提高警覺的認知和教導人們選擇替代方案 。
so whenever possible , to choose alternatives to singleuse plastics .	所以 , 無論何時 , 選擇用到單一塑膠的替代品 。
we can cut the stem tide the stem of this into our oceans and in doing so , save our oceans , save our planet , save ourselves .	我們可以把這首詩切成我們的海洋 , 這樣做 , 拯救我們的海洋 , 拯救我們的地球 , 拯救我們自己 。
this demo from pattie maes' lab at mit , spearheaded by pranav mistry was the buzz of ted . it's a wearable device with a projector that paves the way for profound interaction with our environment . imagine " minority report " and then some .	在麻省理工學院的帕特•馬斯的實驗室 , 被帕拉維•密爾指的是ted的一個可穿戴式裝置 , 一個投影機 , 讓環境深刻的互動 。 想像 「 少數報告 」 和 「 少數性報告 」 。
demo , design , interface design , technology	demo , 設計 , 介面設計 , 科技 , 科技 。
pattie maes and pranav mistry demo sixthsense	帕蒂•馬斯和帕拉夫•帕拉夫•密特摩第六感 。
i've been intrigued by this question of whether we could evolve or develop a sixth sense a sense that would give us seamless access and easy access to metainformation or information that may exist somewhere that may be relevant to help us make the right decision about whatever it is that we're coming across .	我對這個問題很感興趣 , 不論我們能否進化或發展出第六感 , 一種感官 , 能讓我們無縫的接觸、容易取得的資訊 , 或許能協助我們做出正確的決策 , 來協助我們做出正確的決策 。
and some of you may argue , well , don't today's cell phones do that already ?	有些人可能會說 , 嗯 , 今天的手機不是已經做到的嗎 ?
but i would say no .	但我會說 , 不 。
when you meet someone here at ted and this is the top networking place , of course , of the year you don't shake somebody's hand and then say , " can you hold on for a moment while i take out my phone and google you ? "	當你在ted碰到某個人 , 當然是最頂尖的網絡 , 你不會搖著某人的手 , 然後說: 「 你能不能在我拿出手機的時候抓住你嗎 ? 」
or when you go to the supermarket and you're standing there in that huge aisle of different types of toilet papers , you don't take out your cell phone , and open a browser , and go to a website to try to decide which of these different toilet papers is the most ecologically responsible purchase to make .	或當你去超市 , 你站在那一大堆不同的廁所文件中 , 你不會拿出你的手機 , 打開瀏覽器 , 然後去一個網站 , 試著決定這些不同的廁所報紙是最合理的購買法 。
so we don't really have easy access to all this relevant information that can just help us make optimal decisions about what to do next and what actions to take .	所以 , 我們沒有很容易取得相關的資訊 , 只能協助我們做出最佳決定 , 決定下一步要做什麼 , 以及採取行動 。
and so my research group at the media lab has been developing a series of inventions to give us access to this information in a sort of easy way , without requiring that the user changes any of their behavior .	所以 , 我在媒體實驗室的研究小組已經開發了一系列的發明 , 以一種簡單的方式 , 不需要使用者改變他們的行為 。
and i'm here to unveil our latest effort , and most successful effort so far , which is still very much a work in process .	我來這裡是要揭開我們最新的努力 , 到目前為止 , 這種努力仍是非常成功的過程 。
i'm actually wearing the device right now and we've sort of cobbled it together with components that are off the shelf and that , by the way , only cost 350 dollars at this point in time .	我現在正穿著這個裝置 , 我們將它與裝置的零件混合在一起 , 順便一提 , 目前只花了350美元 。
i'm wearing a camera , just a simple webcam , a portable , batterypowered projection system with a little mirror .	我穿著相機 , 只是一個簡單的網路攝影機 , 一個可攜式、電池發射的投影機 , 一個小鏡子 。
these components communicate to my cell phone in my pocket which acts as the communication and computation device .	這些元件通訊到我的口袋裡的手機 , 它是通訊和運算裝置 。
and in the video here we see my student pranav mistry , who's really the genius who's been implementing and designing this whole system .	在這段影片中 , 我們看到我的學生pranav遺產 , 他是實施和設計這整個系統的天才 。
and we see how this system lets him walk up to any surface and start using his hands to interact with the information that is projected in front of him .	我們可以看到這個系統讓他走到任何表面 , 開始用他的手去和他前面投射在他面前的資訊互動 。
the system tracks the four significant fingers .	系統會追蹤四個手指 。
in this case , he's wearing simple marker caps that you may recognize .	在這個案例中 , 他戴著簡單的標記帽 , 你可能認得出來 。
but if you want a more stylish version you could also paint your nails in different colors .	但如果你想要一個更具體的版本 , 你也可以用不同的顏色畫出你的指甲 。
and the camera basically tracks these four fingers and recognizes any gestures that he's making so he can just go to , for example , a map of long beach , zoom in and out , etc .	攝影機基本上追蹤了這四個手指 , 並認出任何他正在製作的姿勢 , 例如 , 長灘的地圖 , 放大 , 等等 。
the system also recognizes iconic gestures such as the " take a picture " gesture , and then takes a picture of whatever is in front of you .	系統也能辨識出有標準的姿勢 , 例如 「 拍照 」 姿勢 , 然後拍攝你面前的任何東西 。
and when he then walks back to the media lab , he can just go up to any wall and project all the pictures that he's taken , sort through them and organize them , and resize them , etc . , again using all natural gestures .	當他回到媒體實驗室時 , 他可以走到任何牆上 , 投影所有他拍攝的照片 , 將它們組織起來 , 再次用所有自然的姿態 。
so , some of you most likely were here two years ago and saw the demo by jeff han or some of you may think , " well , doesn't this look like the microsoft surface table ? "	所以 , 兩年前有些人可能在場 , 看到傑夫•漢斯或有些人可能會想: 「 嗯 , 這不是微軟表面嗎 ? 」
and yes , you also interact using natural gestures , both hands , etc .	是的 , 你也用自然的姿勢互動 , 雙手等等 。
but the difference here is that you can use any surface , you can walk to up to any surface , including your hand if nothing else is available and interact with this projected data .	但這裡的差別是 , 你可以用任何表面 , 你可以走到任何表面 , 包括你的手 , 如果沒有其他東西可以用 , 和這個投影的資料互動 。
the device is completely portable , and can be . . .	這個裝置是完全可攜式的 , 可以是......
so one important difference is that it's totally mobile .	一個重要的差別是它完全是行動 。
another even more important difference is that in mass production this would not cost more tomorrow than today's cell phones and would actually not sort of be a bigger packaging could look a lot more stylish than this version that i'm wearing around my neck .	另一個更重要的差異是 , 在大量生產中 , 明天的成本不會比現今的手機更高 , 實際上 , 包裝不會更大 , 比我在脖子上穿的版本還要多 。
but other than letting some of you live out your fantasy of looking as cool as tom cruise in " minority report , " the reason why we're really excited about this device is that it really can act as one of these sixthsense devices that gives you relevant information about whatever is in front of you .	但 , 除了讓你們之外 , 你們之中 , 看起來很酷 , 在 「 少數民族報告報告 」 中 , 我們對這個裝置的理由是它真的可以作為這六感裝置之一 , 讓你對你面前的任何資訊有相關性 。
so we see pranav here going into the supermarket and he's shopping for some paper towels .	我們看到帕拉病毒進入超市 , 他正在購物一些紙巾 。
and , as he picks up a product the system can recognize the product that he's picking up , using either image recognition or marker technology , and give him the green light or an orange light .	當他拿起一個產品時 , 系統可以辨識出他拿起的產品 , 使用影像辨識或標記技術 , 給他綠光或橘光 。
he can ask for additional information .	他可以請求額外的資訊 。
so this particular choice here is a particularly good choice , given his personal criteria .	這種特定的選擇是特別好的選擇 , 因為他個人的標準 。
some of you may want the toilet paper with the most bleach in it rather than the most ecologicallyresponsible choice .	有些人可能會想要有最多的廁所紙 , 而不是最有責任的選擇 。
if he picks up a book in the bookstore , he can get an amazon rating it gets projected right on the cover of the book .	如果他在書店裡拿起一本書 , 他就可以拿到亞馬遜評分 , 就會在書的封面上投影出來 。
this is juan's book , our previous speaker , which gets a great rating , by the way , at amazon .	這是胡安的書 , 我們先前的演講者 , 順便一提 , 亞馬遜的評級 。
and so , pranav turns the page of the book and can then see additional information about the book reader comments , maybe sort of information by his favorite critic , etc .	所以 , 帕拉夫將這本書的頁面轉變 , 再來看看這本書的讀者評論 , 也許是他最喜歡的批評者的資訊 。
if he turns to a particular page he finds an annotation by maybe an expert of a friend of ours that gives him a little bit of additional information about whatever is on that particular page .	如果他轉到一個特別的頁面 , 他會找到一個朋友的註解 , 給予他一點額外的資訊 , 關於那個頁面的任何資訊 。
reading the newspaper it never has to be outdated .	閱讀報紙永遠不需要太過時了 。
you can get video annotations of the event that you're reading about you can get the latest sports scores etc .	你可以得到你正在閱讀的事件的影片註解 , 你可以得到最新的運動分數等等 。
this is a more controversial one .	這是一個更具爭議性的 。
as you interact with someone at ted , maybe you can see a word cloud of the tags , the words that are associated with that person in their blog and personal web pages .	當你和ted的某個人互動時 , 也許你會看到一個標籤的字 , 和那個人在他們的部落格和個人網頁中連結的字 。
in this case , the student is interested in cameras , etc .	在這個例子中 , 學生對攝影機有興趣 , 等等 。
on your way to the airport , if you pick up your boarding pass , it can tell you that your flight is delayed , that the gate has changed , etc .	在你到機場的路上 , 如果你拿起你的登機 , 它可以告訴你你的飛行裝置被延遲 , 閘門已經改變了 , 等等 。
and , if you need to know what the current time is it's as simple as drawing a watch on your arm .	如果你需要知道目前的時機 , 簡單地在你的手臂上畫手錶 。
so that's where we're at so far in developing this sixth sense that would give us seamless access to all this relevant information about the things that we may come across .	所以 , 到目前為止 , 我們正在發展這六感 , 使我們無法取得所有相關的資訊 , 關於我們可能遇到的事物 。
my student pranav , who's really , like i said , the genius behind this .	我的學生帕拉夫 , 真的很像我說的 , 背後的天才 。
he does deserve a lot of applause because i don't think he's slept much in the last three months , actually .	他的確值得很多掌聲 , 因為我不認為他在過去三個月裡睡得太多了 。
and his girlfriend is probably not very happy about him either .	他的女朋友可能也不太開心 。
but it's not perfect yet , it's very much a work in progress .	但這還不完美 , 進步很多 。
and who knows , maybe in another 10 years we'll be here with the ultimate sixth sense brain implant .	誰知道 , 或許在接下來的十年 , 我們將來會有六感大腦植入 。
phyllis rodriguez and aicha elwafi have a powerful friendship born of unthinkable loss . rodriguez' son was killed in the world trade center attacks on september 11 , 2001 ; elwafi's son zacarias moussaoui was convicted of a role in those attacks and is serving a life sentence . in hoping to find peace , these two moms have come to understand and respect one another .	菲利莎•羅德里格茲和艾瑞莎有一位強大的友誼 , 充滿了不可思議的失去 , 羅德•索維茲的兒子在9月11日被殺害 , 2001年9月11日 , 艾爾菲的兒子•桑卡薩尼在那些攻擊中被判定扮演的角色 , 希望能找到和平 , 這兩位母親來來來來來互相尊敬 。
culture , global issues , politics	文化、全球議題、政治議題、政治議題、
9/11 healing: the mothers who found forgiveness , friendship	911的治癒方式:找到寬恕、友誼、友誼的母親 。
phyllis rodriguez: we are here today because of the fact that we have what most people consider an unusual friendship .	菲利斯•羅德里格茲:我們今天來到這裡 , 因為我們有大多數人認為不尋常的友誼 。
and yet , it feels natural to us now .	然而 , 對我們來說 , 感覺很自然 。
i first learned that my son had been in the world trade center on the morning of september 11th , 2001 .	我第一次了解到 , 我的兒子在2001年9月11日的9月11日貿易中心 。
we didn't know if he had perished yet until 36 hours later .	我們不知道他是否曾在36小時後被判死刑 。
at the time , we knew that it was political .	當時 , 我們知道它是政治的 。
we were afraid of what our country was going to do in the name of our son my husband , orlando , and i and our family .	我們害怕我們的國家會用我兒子的名字 , 奧蘭多 , 我和我們的家人 。
and when i saw it and yet , through the shock , the terrible shock , and the terrible explosion in our lives , literally , we were not vengeful .	當我看到它時 , 經過震驚 , 震驚的震驚 , 以及我們生活中可怕的爆炸 , 真的是 , 我們還沒有復仇 。
and a couple of weeks later when zacarias moussaoui was indicted on six counts of conspiracy to commit terrorism , and the u . s . government called for a death penalty for him , if convicted , my husband and i spoke out in opposition to that , publicly .	幾週後 , 扎卡亞斯•莫薩烏伊被指責犯下恐怖主義 , 美國政府為他打電話給死刑 , 如果被判死刑 , 我先生和我公開對話 。
through that and through human rights groups , we were brought together with several other victims' families .	透過這些人權團體 , 我們和許多其他受害者的家庭聚在一起 。
when i saw aicha in the media , coming over when her son was indicted , and i thought , " what a brave woman .	當我在媒體上看到aicha時 , 她兒子被指控過來 , 我心想: 「 一個勇敢的女人 。
someday i want to meet that woman when i'm stronger . "	有一天 , 我想要在我更強壯的時候見到那個女人 。 」
i was still in deep grief ; i knew i didn't have the strength .	我還在很深的悲傷中 , 我知道我沒有力量 。
i knew i would find her someday , or we would find each other .	我知道有一天我會找到她 , 或我們會找到彼此 。
because , when people heard that my son was a victim , i got immediate sympathy .	因為 , 當人們聽到我的兒子是受害者 , 我立即有同理心 。
but when people learned what her son was accused of , she didn't get that sympathy .	但當人們知道她兒子被指控的是什麼時 , 她並沒有得到那種同理心 。
but her suffering is equal to mine .	但她的痛苦和我一樣 。
so we met in november 2002 , and aicha will now tell you how that came about .	所以 , 我們在2002年11月見面 , aicha現在會告訴你這怎麼回事 。
aicha elwafi: good afternoon , ladies and gentlemen .	aichaelwafi:午安 , 各位先生女士 。
i am the mother of zacarias moussaoui .	我是zacaria的母親 。
and i asked the organization of human rights to put me in touch with the parents of the victims .	我詢問了人權組織 , 讓我與受害者的父母接觸 。
so they introduced me to five families .	他們把我介紹給五個家庭 。
and i saw phyllis , and i watched her .	我看到了phyllis , 我看了她 。
she was the only mother in the group .	她是群體中唯一的母親 。
the others were brothers , sisters .	其他人是兄弟 , 姐妹 。
and i saw in her eyes that she was a mother , just like me .	我在她的眼中看到她是母親 , 就像我一樣 。
i suffered a lot as a mother .	我身為母親 , 受苦很多 。
i was married when i was 14 .	我十四歲時結婚了 。
i lost a child when i was 15 , a second child when i was 16 .	我十五歲時失去了一個孩子 , 我十六歲時 , 第二個孩子 。
so the story with zacarias was too much really .	所以 , zacaria的故事實在太大了 。
and i still suffer , because my son is like he's buried alive .	我仍然感到痛苦 , 因為我兒子就好像被埋葬了一樣 。
i know she really cried for her son .	我知道她真的為她兒子哭了 。
but she knows where he is .	但她知道他在哪裡 。
my son , i don't know where he is .	我的兒子 , 我不知道他在哪裡 。
i don't know if he's alive . i don't know if he's tortured .	我不知道他是否活著 , 我不知道他有沒有被折磨 。
i don't know what happened to him .	我不知道他發生了什麼事 。
so that's why i decided to tell my story , so that my suffering is something positive for other women .	這就是為什麼我決定要說我的故事 , 所以 , 我的痛苦對其他女性來說是正面的 。
for all the women , all the mothers that give life , you can give back , you can change .	所有婦女 , 所有給予生命的母親 , 你可以回饋 , 你可以改變 。
it's up to us women , because we are women , because we love our children .	因為我們是女性 , 因為我們是女性 , 因為我們愛我們的孩子 。
we must be handinhand and do something together .	我們必須雙手做點什麼 。
it's not against women , it's for us , for us women , for our children .	不是對女人 , 而是對我們 , 對我們女性 , 對我們的孩子 。
i talk against violence , against terrorism .	我反對暴力 , 反對恐怖主義 。
i go to schools to talk to young , muslim girls so they don't accept to be married against their will very young .	我去學校跟年輕的穆斯林女孩說話 , 所以她們不接受和她們的意志結婚 。
so if i can save one of the young girls , and avoid that they get married and suffer as much as i did , well this is something good .	所以 , 如果我能拯救其中一位年輕女孩 , 避免她們和我一樣結婚和受苦 , 嗯 , 這是件好事 。
this is why i'm here in front of you .	這就是為什麼我站在你們面前 。
pr: i would like to say that i have learned so much from aicha , starting with that day we had our very first meeting with other family members which was a very private meeting with security , because it was november 2002 , and , frankly , we were afraid of the superpatriotism of that time in the country those of us family members .	pr:我想說 , 我從aicha學到很多 , 從那天開始 , 我們和其他家族成員第一次見面 , 那是一個非常私人的會議 , 因為這是2002年11月 , 坦白說 , 我們害怕那個時候在美國的超父主義 。
but we were all so nervous .	但我們都很緊張 。
" why does she want to meet us ? "	「 為什麼她要見我們 ? 」
and then she was nervous .	然後她又緊張了 。
" why did we want to meet her ? "	「 為什麼我們要見她 ? 」
what did we want from each other ?	我們彼此想要什麼 ?
before we knew each others' names , or anything , we had embraced and wept .	在我們認識彼此的名字之前 , 我們已經擁抱和wept 。
then we sat in a circle with support , with help , from people experienced in this kind of reconciliation .	接著 , 我們在一個充滿支持的圈子裡 , 協助 , 從人們體驗到這種解析 。
and aicha started , and she said , " i don't know if my son is guilty or innocent , but i want to tell you how sorry i am for what happened to your families .	aicha開始 , 她說: 「 我不知道我的兒子有罪或無辜 , 但我想告訴你們 , 我對你的家人有多抱歉 。
i know what it is to suffer , and i feel that if there is a crime , a person should be tried fairly and punished . "	我知道要承受什麼 , 我覺得如果有犯罪 , 一個人應該是公平的、懲罰 。 」
but she reached out to us in that way , and it was , i'd like to say , it was an icebreaker .	但她用這種方式向我們伸出援手 , 我想要說 , 那是個冰箱 。
and what happened then is we all told our stories , and we all connected as human beings .	接下來發生的是 , 我們都告訴我們自己的故事 , 我們都是人的連結 。
by the end of the afternoon it was about three hours after lunch we'd felt as if we'd known each other forever .	到了下午的結束 , 午餐三小時後 , 我們感覺到 , 彷彿我們永遠認識彼此 。
now what i learned from her , is a woman , not only who could be so generous under these present circumstances and what it was then , and what was being done to her son , but the life she's had .	我從她身上學到的是 , 一個女人 , 不僅是她在這些現在的情況下如此慷慨 , 以及她對她的兒子所做的事 , 還有她所擁有的生命 。
i never had met someone with such a hard life , from such a totally different culture and environment from my own .	我從來沒有遇過這麼難過的人 , 從這樣一個完全不同的文化和環境中 。
and i feel that we have a special connection , which i value very much .	我覺得我們有一個特別的連結 , 我非常重視它 。
and i think it's all about being afraid of the other , but making that step and then realizing , " hey , this wasn't so hard .	我覺得這一切都要害怕他人 , 但要讓這一步 , 然後意識到: 「 嘿 , 這並不難 。
who else can i meet that i don't know , or that i'm so different from ? "	我還能碰到我不知道的 , 或是我和誰不同 ? 」
so , aicha , do you have a couple of words for conclusion ?	所以 , aicha , 你有沒有想出幾個字嗎 ?
because our time is up .	因為我們的時間到了 。
aw: i wanted to say that we have to try to know other people , the other .	aw:我想說的是 , 我們必須試著認識他人 , 另一個人 。
you have to be generous , and your hearts must be generous , your mind must be generous .	你必須要慷慨 , 你的心一定要慷慨 , 你的大腦必須要慷慨 。
you must be tolerant .	你一定是堅持的 。
you have to fight against violence .	你必須對抗暴力 。
and i hope that someday we'll all live together in peace and respecting each other .	我希望有一天 , 我們會一起生活在和平和尊重彼此 。
this is what i wanted to say .	這是我想說的 。
too much of the world lacks access to clean drinking water . engineer michael pritchard did something about it inventing the portable lifesaver filter , which can make the most revolting water drinkable in seconds . an amazing demo from tedglobal 2009 .	世界上有太多人無法取得乾淨的飲用水 。 工程師麥可•普里卡 , 發明了可攜式的生物濾水器 , 可以在二零九年tedglobal的tedglobaltedglobal提出一個驚人的示範 。
business , demo , design , global issues , invention , technology , water	商業、demo、設計、全球議題、發明、科技、水資源、水資源、水資源 。
michael pritchard's water filter turns filthy water drinkable	michaelpritchard的水過濾器轉化為骯髒的水飲料 。
i'd like to talk about a couple of things today .	今天我想談談幾件事情 。
the first thing is water .	首先是水 。
now i see you've all been enjoying the water that's been provided for you here at the conference , over the past couple of days .	現在我看到你們都在享受這座研討會為你們提供的水 , 在過去的幾天裡 。
and i'm sure you'll feel that it's from a safe source .	我相信你們會覺得這是安全的來源 。
but what if it wasn't ?	但如果不是這樣呢 ?
what if it was from a source like this ?	如果它來自這樣一個來源呢 ?
then statistics would actually say that half of you would now be suffering with diarrhea .	統計數據會說 , 你們當中有一半會患有腹瀉 。
i talked a lot in the past about statistics , and the provision of safe drinking water for all .	過去我談了很多關於統計數據 , 以及所有人飲用水的建設 。
but they just don't seem to get through .	但它們似乎沒有經過 。
and i think i've worked out why .	我想我已經知道為什麼了 。
it's because , using current thinking , the scale of the problem just seems too huge to contemplate solving .	因為 , 使用目前的思維 , 問題的規模似乎太大了 , 無法思考解決問題 。
so we just switch off: us , governments and aid agencies .	所以我們就關掉:我們、政府和援助機構 。
well , today , i'd like to show you that through thinking differently , the problem has been solved .	今天 , 我想用不同的思考方式來向各位展示 , 問題已經被解決了 。
by the way , since i've been speaking , another 13 , 000 people around the world are suffering now with diarrhea .	順便一提 , 自從我開始說起 , 全世界有一萬三千人罹患腹瀉 。
and four children have just died .	四個孩子剛過世了 。
i invented lifesaver bottle because i got angry .	我發明了救生素瓶 , 因為我生氣了 。
i , like most of you , was sitting down , the day after christmas in 2004 , when i was watching the devastating news of the asian tsunami as it rolled in , playing out on tv .	我和大部分人一樣 , 在2004年聖誕節後的一天 , 當我看著亞洲海嘯的毀滅性消息 , 當時在電視上播放 。
the days and weeks that followed , people fleeing to the hills , being forced to drink contaminated water or face death .	接下來的幾天和幾週 , 人們逃到山丘 , 被迫喝下污染的水或面對死亡 。
that really stuck with me .	這真的讓我困住了 。
then , a few months later , hurricane katrina slammed into the side of america .	接著 , 幾個月後 , 卡崔娜颶風落入美國 。
" okay , " i thought , " here's a first world country , let's see what they can do . "	「 好吧 , 」 我心想: 「 這是第一個世界 , 讓我們看看他們能做什麼 。 」
do you know it took five days to get water to the superdome ?	你知道嗎 ? 要花五天才能讓水到超級室 ?
people were shooting each other on the streets for tv sets and water .	人們在街上為電視節目和水槍擊彼此 。
that's when i decided i had to do something .	那時我決定要做點什麼 。
now i spent a lot of time in my garage , over the next weeks and months , and also in my kitchen much to the dismay of my wife .	現在我花了很多時間在我的車庫裡 , 在接下來的幾週和幾個月 , 我廚房裡也對我妻子感到不安 。
however , after a few failed prototypes , i finally came up with this , the lifesaver bottle .	然而 , 在少數失敗的原型之後 , 我終於想出了這個 , 救命的瓶子 。
okay , now for the science bit .	好吧 , 現在來談談科學 。
before lifesaver , the best hand filters were only capable of filtering down to about 200 nanometers .	在生物樣本之前 , 最好的手過濾器只能過濾到大約200奈米 。
the smallest bacteria is about 200 nanometers .	最小的細菌大約有200奈米 。
so a 200nanometer bacteria is going to get through a 200nanometer hole .	一個200奈米的細菌會穿過200奈米的洞 。
the smallest virus , on the other hand , is about 25 nanometers .	另一方面 , 最小的病毒大約是25奈米 。
so that's definitely going to get through those 200 nanometer holes .	所以這絕對會穿越這兩百奈米大孔 。
lifesaver pores are 15 nanometers .	生命沙龍是15奈米 。
so nothing is getting through .	所以 , 什麼都沒有 。
okay , i'm going to give you a bit of a demonstration .	好 , 我要給你們一些示範 。
would you like to see that ?	你想看到嗎 ?
i spent all the time setting this up , so i guess i should .	我花了很多時間設定這點 , 所以我猜我應該要 。
we're in the fine city of oxford .	我們在牛津城 。
so someone's done that up .	所以 , 有人這樣做 。
fine city of oxford , so what i've done is i've gone and got some water from the river cherwell , and the river thames , that flow through here . and this is the water .	牛津的城市好了 , 所以我做的是 , 我從河流中拿到了一些水 , 河流在這裡流過來 , 這是水 。
but i got to thinking , you know , if we were in the middle of a flood zone in bangladesh , the water wouldn't look like this .	但我想 , 若我們在孟加拉的洪水區中 , 水就不會像這樣 。
so i've gone and got some stuff to add into it .	所以我已經去了 , 把一些東西加進去 。
and this is from my pond .	這是我的池塘 。
have a smell of that , mister cameraman .	試試一下 , 攝影師的氣味 。
we're just going to pour that in there .	我們只是要把它倒進去 。
michael pritchard: okay . we've got some runoff from a sewage plant farm .	michaelprichard:好的 , 我們有一些從污水農場跑出來的 。
so i'm just going to put that in there .	所以 , 我要把它放進去 。
put that in there . there we go .	把它放進去 , 開始吧 。
and some other bits and pieces , chuck that in there .	另外還有一些小片段和碎片 , 卡在裡面 。
and i've got a gift here from a friend of mine's rabbit .	我有一個朋友的兔子的禮物 。
so we're just going to put that in there as well .	所以 , 我們也要把它放進去 。
the lifesaver bottle works really simply .	生物救生素瓶真的很簡單 。
you just scoop the water up .	你只要把水放上去 。
today i'm going to use a jug just to show you all . let's get a bit of that poo in there .	今天我要用一顆果汁給大家看 , 讓大家看一下裡面的小兒子 。
that's not dirty enough . let's just stir that up a little bit .	那還不夠髒 。 咱們來稍微攪拌一下 。
okay , so i'm going to take this really filthy water , and put it in here . do you want a drink yet ?	好 , 所以我要把這個非常骯髒的水放進這裡 , 你要喝嗎 ?
okay . there we go .	好 , 我們開始吧 。
give it a few pumps . okay ?	給你幾個幫浦 , 好嗎 ?
that's all that's necessary .	這是必要的 。
now as soon as i pop the teat , sterile drinking water is going to come out .	一旦我把脂肪抽出來 , 固定的飲用水就會出去 。
i've got to be quick . okay , ready ?	我得很快 , 好 , 準備好了嗎 ?
there we go . mind the electrics .	就這樣 , 請注意電力 。
that is safe , sterile drinking water .	那是安全、穩定的飲用水 。
there you go chris .	克里斯 。
what's it taste of ?	它的味道是什麼 ?
let's see chris's program throughout the rest of the show . okay ?	咱們來看看克里斯在其他節目裡的程式 。 好嗎 ?
okay . lifesaver bottle is used by thousands of people around the world .	好的 , 世界各地有成千上萬的人使用過生命瓶 。
it'll last for 6 , 000 liters .	它會維持六千公升 。
and when it's expired , using failsafe technology , the system will shut off , protecting the user .	當它爆炸時 , 使用失敗的技術 , 系統就會關閉 , 保護使用者 。
pop the cartridge out . pop a new one in .	把這張卡路里趕出去 , 再打個新東西 。
it's good for another 6 , 000 liters .	對另一萬六千公升來說是好的 。
so let's look at the applications .	咱們來看看這個應用 。
traditionally , in a crisis , what do we do ?	傳統上 , 在危機中 , 我們要怎麼做 ?
then , after a few weeks , we set up camps .	然後 , 幾週後 , 我們設立營地 。
and people are forced to come into the camps to get their safe drinking water .	人們被迫進入難民營 , 讓他們的安全飲用水 。
what happens when 20 , 000 people congregate in a camp ?	當兩萬人聚集在營地時會發生什麼事 ?
diseases spread . more resources are required .	疾病散播 , 需要更多資源 。
the problem just becomes selfperpetuating .	問題就變成了自我延續的 。
but by thinking differently , and shipping these , people can stay put .	但藉由不同的思維 , 運送這些資料 , 人們可以留下來 。
they can make their own sterile drinking water , and start to get on with rebuilding their homes and their lives .	他們可以製造自己的穩定飲用水 , 開始重建家園和生活 。
now , it doesn't require a natural disaster for this to work .	這並不需要天然災害才能成功 。
using the old thinking , of national infrastructure and pipe work , is too expensive .	使用舊思維 , 國家基礎建設和管道的工作太昂貴了 。
when you run the numbers on a calculator , you run out of noughts .	當你在計算機上執行數字時 , 你就失敗了 。
so here is the " thinking different " bit .	這裡是 「 思考 」 的位置 。
instead of shipping water , and using manmade processes to do it , let's use mother nature . she's got a fantastic system .	與其運送水 , 使用人造的流程 , 讓我們使用大自然 。 她有一個很棒的系統 。
she picks the water up from there , desalinates it , for free , transports it over there , and dumps it onto the mountains , rivers , and streams .	她從那裡拿起水 , 免費送到那裡 , 把水丟到山上 , 河流和溪流上 。
and where do people live ? near water .	人們住在哪裡 ? 鄰近水域 。
all we've go to do is make it sterile . how do we do that ?	我們所要做的就是讓它穩定 , 我們要怎麼做 ?
well , we could use the lifesaver bottle .	嗯 , 我們可以用生物樣本 。
or we could use one of these .	或者 , 我們可以用其中一種 。
the same technology , in a jerry can .	同樣的技術 , 在jerry能做到的 。
this will process 25 , 000 liters of water ; that's good enough for a family of four , for three years .	這會處理二萬五千公升的水 ; 足夠四個家庭 , 三年之久 。
and how much does it cost ?	要花多少錢 ?
about half a cent a day to run .	一天大概只有半分錢才能經營 。
so , by thinking differently , and processing water at the point of use , mothers and children no longer have to walk four hours a day to collect their water .	所以 , 用不同的方式思考和處理水 , 母親和孩子不再需要每天走四小時才能收集他們的水 。
they can get it from a source nearby .	它們可以從附近的來源取得 。
so with just eight billion dollars , we can hit the millennium goal's target of halving the number of people without access to safe drinking water .	只要花了八十億美金 , 我們就能達到千禧年目標 , 來拯救人們的數量 , 不用取得安全的飲用水 。
to put that into context , the u . k . government spends about 12 billion pounds a year on foreign aid .	以此為背景 , 英國政府每年花大約120億英鎊在外國援助 。
but why stop there ?	但為什麼要停下來 ?
with 20 billion dollars , everyone can have access to safe drinking water .	有200億美元 , 每個人都能取得安全飲用水 。
so the threeandahalf billion people that suffer every year as a result , and the two million kids that die every year , will live .	所以每年有三千五億人遭受痛苦 , 每年有兩百萬個孩子死去 , 會活下來 。
paddy ashdown claims that we are living in a moment in history where power is changing in ways it never has before . in a spellbinding talk at tedxbrussels he outlines the three major global shifts that he sees coming .	padadyshown聲稱我們生活在歷史上 , 權力在以前從未有過的方式改變 。 在tedxussel的演講中他提到他所見到的三個重大的全球轉變
foreign policy , global issues , politics , world cultures	外交政策、全球議題、政治、世界文化、文化 。
paddy ashdown: the global power shift	padyshown:全球權力的轉變 。
there's a poem written by a very famous english poet at the end of the 19th century .	在十九世紀末 , 有一首詩寫了一首著名的英文詩 。
it was said to echo in churchill's brain in the 1930s .	在1930年代 , 它被用來回應教堂的大腦 。
and the poem goes: " on the idle hill of summer , lazy with the flow of streams , hark i hear a distant drummer , drumming like a sound in dreams , far and near and low and louder on the roads of earth go by , dear to friend and food to powder , soldiers marching , soon to die . "	這首詩是: 「 在夏天的大山上 , 充滿著溪流的流動 , 我聽到一個遙遠的鼓聲 , 鼓聲就像是夢中的聲音 , 很近、很低、很大聲 , 在地球的路上 , 親愛的朋友 , 吃粉、食物、士兵遊行 , 很快就死亡 。 」
those who are interested in poetry , the poem is " a shropshire lad " written by a . e . housman .	那些對詩很感興趣的人 , 這首詩是 " 夏洛夫拉 " 由a.e.housman所寫的 。
but what housman understood , and you hear it in the symphonies of nielsen too , was that the long , hot , silvan summers of stability of the 19th century were coming to a close , and that we were about to move into one of those terrifying periods of history when power changes .	但霍斯曼也知道 , 在尼爾森的交響樂中 , 你也聽到這句話 , 那就是 , 十九世紀的穩定性夏天的穩定性 , 我們即將進入一個可怕的時代 , 當權力改變 。
and these are always periods , ladies and gentlemen , accompanied by turbulence , and all too often by blood .	女士們 , 女士們先生們 , 伴隨著亂流 , 經常是血液 。
and my message for you is that i believe we are condemned , if you like , to live at just one of those moments in history when the gimbals upon which the established order of power is beginning to change and the new look of the world , the new powers that exist in the world , are beginning to take form .	而我的訊息是 , 我相信我們是有信心的 , 如果你喜歡 , 在歷史上 , 最高階級的權力開始改變世界的新角度 , 世界上存在的新勢力開始開始形成 。
and these are and we see it very clearly today nearly always highly turbulent times , highly difficult times , and all too often very bloody times .	今天我們看到的很明顯 , 幾乎永遠都很亂 , 很困難的時刻 , 很多時候都太過血 。
by the way , it happens about once every century .	順便一提 , 每一世紀都發生一次 。
you might argue that the last time it happened and that's what housman felt coming and what churchill felt too was that when power passed from the old nations , the old powers of europe , across the atlantic to the new emerging power of the united states of america the beginning of the american century .	你可能會爭辯說 , 上次發生了這場演說 , 霍斯曼感來了 , 以及教會的感受 , 就是當權力從古老的國家通過 , 歐洲的舊勢力 , 橫跨大西洋到美國新興的新興力量 , 美國一世紀開始的新興力量 。
and of course , into the vacuum where the tooold european powers used to be were played the two bloody catastrophes of the last century the one in the first part and the one in the second part: the two great world wars .	當然 , 在真空中歐洲的權力 , 以前的兩場血腥的災難 , 發生在上個世紀的兩場災難 , 第二部分:二場大戰 。
mao zedong used to refer to them as the european civil wars , and it's probably a more accurate way of describing them .	maozedong用來當歐洲內戰時 , 它可能是更精確的描述方式 。
well , ladies and gentlemen , we live at one of those times .	各位先生女士 , 我們生活在其中之一 。
but for us , i want to talk about three factors today .	但對我們來說 , 我今天要談三個因子 。
and the first of these , the first two of these , is about a shift in power .	首先 , 這兩者是權力的轉變 。
and the second is about some new dimension which i want to refer to , which has never quite happened in the way it's happening now .	第二個是關於一些新的維度 , 我想要提出一個新的維度 , 目前從來沒有發生過 。
but let's talk about the shifts of power that are occurring to the world .	但讓我們來談談在世界發生權力的轉變 。
and what is happening today is , in one sense , frightening because it's never happened before .	今天發生的狀況是 , 很害怕 , 因為從來沒有發生過 。
we have seen lateral shifts of power the power of greece passed to rome and the power shifts that occurred during the european civilizations but we are seeing something slightly different .	我們已經看到了革命的力量 , 希臘的力量過去了羅馬的力量 , 以及在歐洲文明期間發生的權力轉移 , 但我們看到一些稍微不同的東西 。
for power is not just moving laterally from nation to nation .	權力不僅僅是以後從國家到國家的移動 。
it's also moving vertically .	它也在垂直移動 。
what's happening today is that the power that was encased , held to accountability , held to the rule of law , within the institution of the nation state has now migrated in very large measure onto the global stage .	現今正在發生的力量是 , 負責責任的權力 , 在國家國家的制度中 , 已經在全球階段大規模的測量方式上移民 。
the globalization of power we talk about the globalization of markets , but actually it's the globalization of real power .	全球化的權力 , 我們談的是市場化 , 但實際上是全球化的權力 。
and where , at the nation state level that power is held to accountability subject to the rule of law , on the international stage it is not .	在國際層面上 , 權力被要求為法律規則 , 國際舞台主題 , 不是 。
the international stage and the global stage where power now resides: the power of the internet , the power of the satellite broadcasters , the power of the money changers this vast moneygoround that circulates now 32 times the amount of money necessary for the trade it's supposed to be there to finance the money changers , if you like , the financial speculators that have brought us all to our knees quite recently , the power of the multinational corporations now developing budgets often bigger than mediumsized countries .	國際舞台和全球舞台現在的權力是網際網路的力量 , 衛星廣播的權力 , 金錢改變者的權力 , 這種巨大的金錢場所現在是32倍交易所必要的金錢是金融變革者 , 如果你喜歡 , 金融的推論者 , 把我們所有人帶到我們的膝蓋裡 , 近期 , 跨國企業的權力 , 經常發展出比中國家更大的電力 。
these live in a global space which is largely unregulated , not subject to the rule of law , and in which people may act free of constraint .	這些生活在一個很大的全球空間 , 不受法律規則的主宰 , 而人們可能是免費的限制 。
now that suits the powerful up to a moment .	這套裝置有力到一個時刻 。
it's always suitable for those who have the most power to operate in spaces without constraint , but the lesson of history is that , sooner or later , unregulated space space not subject to the rule of law becomes populated , not just by the things you wanted international trade , the internet , etc . but also by the things you don't want international criminality , international terrorism .	總是適合那些在沒有限制的空間中最有權力的人 , 但歷史的教訓是 , 很快的 , 沒有規範的空間 , 不單單單單單單是你想要國際貿易、網路等等 。 也是你不想要國際犯罪、國際恐怖主義 。
the revelation of 9/11 is that even if you are the most powerful nation on earth , nevertheless , those who inhabit that space can attack you even in your most iconic of cities one bright september morning .	911事件的啟示是 , 即使你是地球上最強大的國家 , 儘管如此 , 那些居住空間的人 , 甚至可以攻擊你大部分的城市 , 一個明亮的九月早晨 。
it's said that something like 60 percent of the four million dollars that was taken to fund 9/11 actually passed through the institutions of the twin towers which 9/11 destroyed .	據說 , 400萬美金大約有60%的資金被帶到911恐怖組織中 , 通過了雙胞胎塔的機構 , 911事件摧毀了 。
you see , our enemies also use this space the space of mass travel , the internet , satellite broadcasters to be able to get around their poison , which is about destroying our systems and our ways .	你看 , 我們的敵人也使用這個空間 , 質量旅行、網路、衛星廣播 , 以取得它們的毒害 , 重點在於摧毀我們的系統和我們的方式 。
sooner or later , sooner or later , the rule of history is that where power goes governance must follow .	不久後 , 歷史的規則是 , 權力的管理必須追隨 。
and if it is therefore the case , as i believe it is , that one of the phenomenon of our time is the globalization of power , then it follows that one of the challenges of our time is to bring governance to the global space .	因此 , 假如我相信 , 我們這個時代的一個現象是全球化的權力 , 那麼 , 我們這個時代的挑戰之一就是把治理帶到全球空間 。
and i believe that the decades ahead of us now will be to a greater or lesser extent turbulent the more or less we are able to achieve that aim: to bring governance to the global space .	我相信 , 未來的數十年將會是更大、更大、更少的亂流 , 我們能夠達成目標:把治理帶到全球空間 。
now notice , i'm not talking about government .	請注意 , 我不是在說政府 。
i'm not talking about setting up some global democratic institution .	我不是在說建立一些全球民主制度 。
my own view , by the way , ladies and gentlemen , is that this is unlikely to be done by spawning more u . n . institutions .	順便一提 , 我自己的觀點 , 女士們先生們 , 這種觀點是不太可能的 , 藉由擴展更多聯合國機構 。
if we didn't have the u . n . , we'd have to invent it .	如果我們沒有聯合國 , 我們就得發明它 。
the world needs an international forum .	世界需要國際論壇 。
it needs a means by which you can legitimize international action .	它需要一種方式 , 讓你可以合法化國際行動 。
but when it comes to governance of the global space , my guess is this won't happen through the creation of more u . n . institutions .	但當談到全球空間的治理時 , 我猜這不會發生 , 透過創造更多聯合國的機構 。
it will actually happen by the powerful coming together and making treatybased systems , treatybased agreements , to govern that global space .	它會發生在強大的團結在一起 , 建立合約的系統、合約的協議、治理全球空間的協議 。
and if you look , you can see them happening , already beginning to emerge .	如果你看 , 你可以看到他們正在發生 , 已經開始出現了 。
the world trade organization: treatybased organization , entirely treatybased , and yet , powerful enough to hold even the most powerful , the united states , to account if necessary .	世界貿易組織:以合約為基礎的組織 , 完全是合法的組織 , 然而 , 強大的力量 , 足以支撐最強大的美國 , 如果必要的話 。
kyoto: the beginnings of struggling to create a treatybased organization .	kyoto:努力奮鬥的開始 , 來建立一個合約的組織 。
the g20: we know now that we have to put together an institution which is capable of bringing governance to that financial space for financial speculation .	g20:我們現在知道 , 我們得要建立一個機構 , 能夠將治理帶入金融空間 , 來推測財務規範 。
and that's what the g20 is , a treatybased institution .	而g20就是以合約為基礎的機構 。
now there's a problem there , and we'll come back to it in a minute , which is that if you bring the most powerful together to make the rules in treatybased institutions , to fill that governance space , then what happens to the weak who are left out ?	現在有一個問題 , 我們等一下會再回到這個問題 , 那就是 , 如果你把最強大的統治規則 , 以合約為基礎的制度來填補那個治理空間 , 會發生什麼事 ?
and that's a big problem , and we'll return to it in just a second .	這是個很大的問題 , 只要一秒鐘就回來了 。
so there's my first message , that if you are to pass through these turbulent times more or less turbulently , then our success in doing that will in large measure depend on our capacity to bring sensible governance to the global space .	所以 , 我的第一個訊息是 , 如果你能通過這些亂流的次數 , 或更少的亂流 , 那麼我們的成功會取決於我們的能力 , 來將全球空間的負面治理帶給我們 。
and watch that beginning to happen .	看著這一切開始發生 。
my second point is , and i know i don't have to talk to an audience like this about such a thing , but power is not just shifting vertically , it's also shifting horizontally .	我的第二點是 , 我知道 , 我不需要和像這樣的觀眾談話 , 而是權力不只在垂直轉移 , 它也在地平地轉移 。
you might argue that the story , the history of civilizations , has been civilizations gathered around seas with the first ones around the mediterranean , the more recent ones in the ascendents of western power around the atlantic .	你可能會爭論這個故事 , 文明的歷史 , 已經在海中聚集在一起 , 帶著第一批在地中海 , 最近在大西洋的西方力量 。
well it seems to me that we're now seeing a fundamental shift of power , broadly speaking , away from nations gathered around the atlantic [seaboard] to the nations gathered around the pacific rim .	對我來說 , 我們現在看到了權力的基本轉變 , 廣泛地說話 , 從大西洋到大西洋的各國都聚集在太平洋中 。
now that begins with economic power , but that's the way it always begins .	從經濟力量開始 , 但這一直是這樣開始的 。
you already begin to see the development of foreign policies , the augmentation of military budgets occurring in the other growing powers in the world .	你已經開始看到外交政策的發展 , 軍事預算的擴增 , 在世界上其他成長的權力 。
i think actually this is not so much a shift from the west to the east ; something different is happening .	其實這不是西方的轉變 , 和東方的轉變 ; 不同的事情正在發生 。
my guess is , for what it's worth , is that the united states will remain the most powerful nation on earth for the next 10 years , 15 , but the context in which she holds her power has now radically altered ; it has radically changed .	我的猜測是 , 值得的 , 美國將會在未來十年內維持著世界上最強大的國家 , 十五年、十五歲 , 但她認為她的權力現在已經徹底改變了 ; 它已經徹底改變了 。
we are coming out of 50 years , most unusual years , of history in which we have had a totally monopolar world , in which every compass needle for or against has to be referenced by its position to washington a world bestrode by a single colossus .	我們從50年以來 , 最不尋常的歷史中 , 我們有一個完全獨立的世界 , 在這個世界中 , 每一位羅盤針 , 都必須被它的位置給華盛頓 , 一個世界最好的英雄 。
but that's not a usual case in history .	但這不是歷史上常見的案例 。
in fact , what's now emerging is the much more normal case of history .	事實上 , 現在正在發生的是更正常的歷史案例 。
you're beginning to see the emergence of a multipolar world .	你正開始看到一個多向分化世界的出現 。
up until now , the united states has been the dominant feature of our world .	到目前為止 , 美國一直是世界的主要特徵 。
they will remain the most powerful nation , but they will be the most powerful nation in an increasingly multipolar world .	他們將維持著最強大的國家 , 但他們將成為一個越來越多世界中最強大的國家 。
and you begin to see the alternative centers of power building up in china , of course , though my own guess is that china's ascent to greatness is not smooth .	而你開始看到中國的權力中心 , 當然 , 我自己的猜測是中國對偉大的中心 , 不是光滑 。
it's going to be quite grumpy as china begins to democratize her society after liberalizing her economy .	中國會開始民主化她的社會 , 在自由化經濟之後 , 自由化了她的社會 。
but that's a subject of a different discussion .	但這是個不同的討論主題 。
you see india , you see brazil .	你看到印度 , 你看到巴西 。
you see increasingly that the world now looks actually , for us europeans , much more like europe in the 19th century .	你可以看到現在世界看起來 , 對歐洲人來說 , 實際上 , 對歐洲人來說 , 比較像19世紀的歐洲 。
europe in the 19th century: a great british foreign secretary , lord canning , used to describe it as the " european concert of powers . "	在十九世紀 , 一個偉大的英國外交部長 , 林肯 , 以前用來描述它是 「 歐洲權力協會 」 。
there was a balance , a fivesided balance .	有平衡 , 五大的平衡 。
britain always played to the balance .	英國總是在平衡上演 。
if paris got together with berlin , britain got together with vienna and rome to provide a counterbalance .	如果巴黎和柏林合作 , 英國和維也納和羅馬一起合作 , 來提供平衡 。
now notice , in a period which is dominated by a monopolar world , you have fixed alliances nato , the warsaw pact .	請注意 , 在一個單一世界主導的時期 , 你已經修復了雙方的盟友 , 戰役的先鋒 。
a fixed polarity of power means fixed alliances .	一個固定的權力的極端代表固定的盟友 。
but a multiple polarity of power means shifting and changing alliances .	但權力的多極限意味著轉變和改變盟友 。
and that's the world we're coming into , in which we will increasingly see that our alliances are not fixed .	這是我們進入的世界 , 我們會越來越常見到我們的盟友並不固定 。
canning , the great british foreign secretary once said , " britain has a common interest , but no common allies . "	坎昆 , 偉大的英國國外秘書長曾說: 「 英國有共同的利益 , 但沒有共同盟友 。 」
and we will see increasingly that even we in the west will reach out , have to reach out , beyond the cozy circle of the atlantic powers to make alliances with others if we want to get things done in the world .	我們會發現 , 即使在西方也能接觸到 , 必須要伸出援手 , 超越大西洋力量的結盟 , 才能和他人聯盟 , 如果我們想要在世界上做事 。
note , that when we went into libya , it was not good enough for the west to do it alone ; we had to bring others in .	請注意 , 當我們走進利比亞時 , 西方不夠好 , 我們得把其他人帶進去 。
we had to bring , in this case , the arab league in .	我們得把阿拉伯聯盟帶進來 。
my guess is iraq and afghanistan are the last times when the west has tried to do it themselves , and we haven't succeeded .	我的猜測是伊拉克和阿富汗 , 西方國家試圖自己做到 , 我們還沒成功 。
my guess is that we're reaching the beginning of the end of 400 years i say 400 years because it's the end of the ottoman empire of the hegemony of western power , western institutions and western values .	我的猜測是400年後的開始 , 我說了400年 , 因為那是西方力量的奧圖曼帝國的終結 , 西方的機構和西方的價值觀 。
you know , up until now , if the west got its act together , it could propose and dispose in every corner of the world .	你知道嗎 , 直到現在 , 如果西方國家團結起來 , 它可以在世界上的每個角落提出和消滅 。
but that's no longer true .	但這已經不是真的了 。
take the last financial crisis after the second world war .	以第二次世界大戰後最後一次金融危機為例 。
the west got together the bretton woods institution , world bank , international monetary fund the problem solved .	西方世界銀行 , 國際貨幣基金解決了問題 。
now we have to call in others .	現在我們必須呼籲他人 。
now we have to create the g20 .	現在我們必須創造g20 。
now we have to reach beyond the cozy circle of our western friends .	現在我們必須超越西方朋友的瘋狂圈 。
let me make a prediction for you , which is probably even more startling .	讓我為你們做一個預測 , 可能更令人驚訝 。
i suspect we are now reaching the end of 400 years when western power was enough .	我猜我們現在已經到了400年的終點 , 西方的權力足夠 。
people say to me , " the chinese , of course , they'll never get themselves involved in peacemaking , multilateral peacemaking around the world . "	人們對我說: 「 中國 , 當然 , 他們永遠不會涉及到和平、多邊和平的交流 。 」
oh yes ? why not ?	是的 ? 為何不呢 ?
how many chinese troops are serving under the blue beret , serving under the blue flag , serving under the u . n . command in the world today ?	有多少中國軍隊在藍色的賭場下 , 在藍色旗幟下 , 在聯合國的指令下 , 服務全世界的國家 ?
how many americans ? 11 .	有多少美國人 ? 十一歲 。
what is the largest naval contingent tackling the issue of somali pirates ?	何謂索馬利海盜最大的海軍聯盟 ?
the chinese naval contingent .	中國的海軍聯盟 。
of course they are , they are a mercantilist nation .	當然 , 他們是農民國家 。
they want to keep the sea lanes open .	他們想讓海道打開 。
increasingly , we are going to have to do business with people with whom we do not share values , but with whom , for the moment , we share common interests .	漸漸地 , 我們要和我們沒有共享價值的人做生意 , 但和誰一起 , 我們共享共同的利益 。
it's a whole new different way of looking at the world that is now emerging .	這是一種全新的看待世界的方式 , 一種現在正在興起的世界 。
and here's the third factor , which is totally different .	第三個因素完全不同 。
today in our modern world , because of the internet , because of the kinds of things people have been talking about here , everything is connected to everything .	今天 , 在我們現代的世界裡 , 由於網際網路 , 因為人們在談論的各種事物 , 一切都與所有事物連結在一起 。
we are now interdependent .	我們現在是互相依賴的 。
we are now interlocked , as nations , as individuals , in a way which has never been the case before , never been the case before .	我們現在被關閉了 , 作為一個國家 , 一個從未發生過的案例 , 從未發生過 。
the interrelationship of nations , well it's always existed .	國家的相互關聯 , 嗯 , 總是存在著 。
diplomacy is about managing the interrelationship of nations .	外交的重點是要管理國家的相互關係 。
but now we are intimately locked together .	但現在 , 我們密切關連在一起了 。
you get swine flu in mexico , it's a problem for charles de gaulle airport 24 hours later .	你在墨西哥得到了瑞士流感 , 那是24小時後 , 查爾斯•德蓋爾機場的問題 。
lehman brothers goes down , the whole lot collapses .	雷曼兄弟掉下來 , 很多崩盤 。
there are fires in the steppes of russia , food riots in africa .	在俄羅斯、非洲的食物暴動中有火 。
we are all now deeply , deeply , deeply interconnected .	我們現在都非常、非常、非常緊密地相互連結 。
and what that means is the idea of a nation state acting alone , not connected with others , not working with others , is no longer a viable proposition .	這意味著 , 一個國家單獨行動的概念 , 而不是與他人連結 , 而不是與他人合作 , 不再是一個可行的建議 。
because the actions of a nation state are neither confined to itself , nor is it sufficient for the nation state itself to control its own territory , because the effects outside the nation state are now beginning to affect what happens inside them .	因為一個國家的行動 , 不只限於自己 , 也不足以控制國家自身的領土 , 因為國家的影響已經開始影響到國家內部的狀況 。
i was a young soldier in the last of the small empire wars of britain .	我是英國最後一場小型帝國戰爭的士兵 。
at that time , the defense of my country was about one thing and one thing only: how strong was our army , how strong was our air force , how strong was our navy and how strong were our allies .	那時 , 我國家的防禦是一件事 , 只有一件事:我們的軍隊有多強壯 , 我們的空軍有多強壯 , 我們的海軍有多強壯 , 我們的盟友有多強壯 。
that was when the enemy was outside the walls .	那時候 , 敵人就在牆外 。
now the enemy is inside the walls .	敵人就在牆上 。
now if i want to talk about the defense of my country , i have to speak to the minister of health because pandemic disease is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of agriculture because food security is a threat to my security , i have to speak to the minister of industry because the fragility of our hitech infrastructure is now a point of attack for our enemies as we see from cyber warfare i have to speak to the minister of home affairs because who has entered my country , who lives in that terraced house in that inner city has a direct effect on what happens in my country as we in london saw in the 7/7 bombings .	現在 , 如果我想要談我國家的防禦 , 我得要和那些健康的部長談 , 因為流行疾病對我的安全有威脅 , 我得要和農業部談談 , 因為食物安全對我的安全是威脅 , 我得要和工業部談談 , 因為我們僱用基礎設施的脆弱 , 正是我們從網路戰爭中看到的敵人 , 我必須對國內的敵人說話 , 我得要和國內的家裡的家鄉 , 談談談 , 因為在我國內 , 第七個家庭中 , 七個案例 。
it's no longer the case that the security of a country is simply a matter for its soldiers and its ministry of defense .	不再是國家安全的案例 , 只是對其士兵和國防部而言是很重要的 。
it's its capacity to lock together its institutions .	是它的能力 , 把它的機構鎖在一起 。
and this tells you something very important .	這告訴我們一件非常重要的事 。
it tells you that , in fact , our governments , vertically constructed , constructed on the economic model of the industrial revolution vertical hierarchy , specialization of tasks , command structures have got the wrong structures completely .	它告訴你 , 事實上 , 我們的政府 , 垂直建構 , 建構在工業革命的經濟模式上 , 垂直的階級制度 , 專門化任務 , 指揮結構完全是錯誤的結構 。
you in business know that the paradigm structure of our time , ladies and gentlemen , is the network .	你在商業界知道我們時代的範式結構 , 各位先生女士 , 是網路 。
it's your capacity to network that matters , both within your governments and externally .	是你對網絡有影響的能力 , 兩者都在你的政府和外部 。
so here is ashdown's third law .	這裡是阿什德欠第三條法則 。
by the way , don't ask me about ashdown's first law and second law because i haven't invented those yet ; it always sounds better if there's a third law , doesn't it ?	順便一提 , 不要問我第一個法律和第二定律 , 因為我還沒有發明這些法則 ; 如果有第三個法則 , 聽起來會比較好嗎 ?
ashdown's third law is that in the modern age , where everything is connected to everything , the most important thing about what you can do is what you can do with others .	ashdown第三個法則是 , 在現代 , 每件事都連接到任何東西 , 最重要的是你能做什麼 , 就是你能和別人做些什麼 。
the most important bit about your structure whether you're a government , whether you're an army regiment , whether you're a business is your docking points , your interconnectors , your capacity to network with others .	你的結構最重要的一點是 , 無論你是政府 , 無論你是軍隊註冊 , 不論你是生意 , 你的交錯點 , 你的連結者 , 你的能力 , 你和其他人的連結 。
you understand that in industry ; governments don't .	你明白在工業界 , 政府沒有 。
but now one final thing .	但現在 , 最後一件事 。
if it is the case , ladies and gentlemen and it is that we are now locked together in a way that has never been quite the same before , then it's also the case that we share a destiny with each other .	如果是這樣的例子 , 女士們先生們 , 我們現在被鎖在一個以前從未相同的方式上 , 那也是我們彼此的命運 。
suddenly and for the very first time , collective defense , the thing that has dominated us as the concept of securing our nations , is no longer enough .	突然間 , 一開始 , 集體防禦 , 把我們當作是保障國家的概念 , 已經不再夠了 。
it used to be the case that if my tribe was more powerful than their tribe , i was safe ; if my country was more powerful than their country , i was safe ; my alliance , like nato , was more powerful than their alliance , i was safe .	以前 , 如果我的部落比他們的部落更強大 , 我是安全的 ; 如果我的國家比他們的國家更強大 , 我是安全的 ; 猶太人 , 像娜托 , 比他們的盟友更強大 , 我是安全的 。
it is no longer the case .	不再是事實 。
the advent of the interconnectedness and of the weapons of mass destruction means that , increasingly , i share a destiny with my enemy .	相互連結的進展和大規模毀滅的武器意味著越來越多 , 我和我的敵人分享了命運 。
when i was a diplomat negotiating the disarmament treaties with the soviet union in geneva in the 1970s , we succeeded because we understood we shared a destiny with them .	我當時是一位外交官協商在1970年代在日內瓦的蘇聯協商時 , 我們成功了 , 因為我們知道我們和他們分享了命運 。
collective security is not enough .	集體安全還不夠 。
peace has come to northern ireland because both sides realized that the zerosum game couldn't work .	和平來到北愛爾蘭 , 因為兩方都知道 , 零和的遊戲是行不通的 。
they shared a destiny with their enemies .	他們和敵人分享了命運 。
one of the great barriers to peace in the middle east is that both sides , both israel and , i think , the palestinians , do not understand that they share a collective destiny .	中東和平的最大障礙之一 , 就是以色列和伊斯蘭人 , 我認為 , 巴勒斯坦人並不了解他們有共同的命運 。
and so suddenly , ladies and gentlemen , what has been the proposition of visionaries and poets down the ages becomes something we have to take seriously as a matter of public policy .	所以 , 女士們先生們 , 一直以來 , 遠見和詩人的提議變成了我們必須認真看待的公共政策 。
i started with a poem , i'll end with one .	我從一首詩開始 , 我會用一首詩來結束 。
the great poem of john donne's .	約翰•唐恩的偉大詩 。
" send not for whom the bell tolls . "	「 不要寄錢給誰 。 」
the poem is called " no man is an island . "	這首詩叫做 「 沒有人是島嶼 」 。
and it goes: " every man's death affected me , for i am involved in mankind , send not to ask for whom the bell tolls , it tolls for thee . "	內容是: 「 每個人的死亡都影響著我 , 因為我在人身上 , 不去尋求任何人的肚子 , 它會為我冒險 。 」
for john donne , a recommendation of morality .	對約翰•唐恩來說 , 是道德的建議 。
for us , i think , part of the equation for our survival .	對我們來說 , 我認為 , 我們生存的一部分 。
to find the path to long life and health , dan buettner and team study the world's " blue zones , " communities whose elders live with vim and vigor to recordsetting age . at tedxtc , he shares the 9 common diet and lifestyle habits that keep them spry past age 100 .	為了尋找長壽和健康的路徑 , 丹•布特納和團隊研究這個世界的 「 藍色區塊 」 , 他們的長輩們和vimorgor一起生活 , 記錄tedxtc的時代 , 他分享了9個常見飲食和生活習慣 , 使他們能在一百歲之前長壽 。
biology , culture , exploration , food , health , life , science	生物、文化、探索、探索、食物、健康、生命、科學、科學、科學 。
dan buettner: how to live to be 100+	丹•布特納:如何活到一百個+ 。
something called the danish twin study established that only about 10 percent of how long the average person lives , within certain biological limits , is dictated by our genes .	一個叫danishwin的研究指出 , 平均壽命的百分之十 , 在某些生物限制下 , 被我們的基因所分離 。
the other 90 percent is dictated by our lifestyle .	其它90%是由我們的生活方式來決定 。
so the premise of blue zones: if we can find the optimal lifestyle of longevity we can come up with a de facto formula for longevity .	所以藍色區域的前提是:如果我們能找到長壽的最佳生活方式 , 我們就能找到一個事實公式 , 長壽的公式 。
but if you ask the average american what the optimal formula of longevity is , they probably couldn't tell you .	但如果你問一般美國人 , 長壽最佳的公式 , 他們可能會不會告訴你 。
they've probably heard of the south beach diet , or the atkins diet .	他們可能聽說過南海灘飲食 , 或墨水飲食 。
you have the usda food pyramid .	你有美國食品藥物管理局 。
there is what oprah tells us .	歐普拉告訴我們什麼 。
there is what doctor oz tells us .	奧茲醫生告訴我們什麼 。
the fact of the matter is there is a lot of confusion around what really helps us live longer better .	事實是 , 有很多困惑 , 真正能幫助我們活得更久 。
should you be running marathons or doing yoga ?	你應該要跑馬拉松或做瑜伽嗎 ?
should you eat organic meats or should you be eating tofu ?	你應該吃有機肉還是吃豆子嗎 ?
when it comes to supplements , should you be taking them ?	談到補給品時 , 你應該要服用他們嗎 ?
how about these hormones or resveratrol ?	荷爾蒙或反轉荷爾蒙呢 ?
and does purpose play into it ?	目的是什麼 ?
spirituality ? and how about how we socialize ?	靈性 ? 我們如何社交呢 ?
well , our approach to finding longevity was to team up with national geographic , and the national institute on aging , to find the four demographically confirmed areas that are geographically defined .	我們尋找長壽的方法是和國家地理學團隊合作 , 國家老化研究所 , 找出四個人口統一的區域 , 確認地理上的定義 。
and then bring a team of experts in there to methodically go through exactly what these people do , to distill down the crosscultural distillation .	接著 , 把一組專家帶到那裡 , 以正常的方式來處理這些人的做法 , 把跨文化分散 。
and at the end of this i'm going to tell you what that distillation is .	最後我要告訴各位 , 這種分析是什麼 。
but first i'd like to debunk some common myths when it comes to longevity .	但 , 首先 , 我想在長壽時破壞一些常見的迷思 。
and the first myth is if you try really hard you can live to be 100 .	第一個迷思是 , 如果你真的很難活到一百歲 。
the problem is , only about one out of 5 , 000 people in america live to be 100 .	問題是 , 美國只有五千人當中只有一人活到一百歲 。
your chances are very low .	你的機會非常低 。
even though it's the fastest growing demographic in america , it's hard to reach 100 .	雖然它是美國成長最快的人口統計 , 但很難達到100 。
the problem is that we're not programmed for longevity .	問題是 , 我們不是為了長壽而設計出來的 。
we are programmed for something called procreative success .	我們為所謂的 「 積極的成功 」 設計出來 。
i love that word .	我喜歡這個詞 。
it reminds me of my college days .	它讓我想起我大學的日子 。
biologists term procreative success to mean the age where you have children and then another generation , the age when your children have children .	生物學家稱之為 「 繁衍的成功 」 , 意思是 「 年齡 」 和 「 孩子 」 的年齡 。
after that the effect of evolution completely dissipates .	在那之後 , 演化的效應完全消失了 。
if you're a mammal , if you're a rat or an elephant , or a human , in between , it's the same story .	如果你是哺乳類 , 如果你是一隻老鼠或一隻大象 , 在兩者之間 , 都是同一個故事 。
so to make it to age 100 , you not only have to have had a very good lifestyle , you also have to have won the genetic lottery .	所以 , 要讓它活到一百歲 , 你不需要有很棒的生活方式 , 你也得贏得基因彩票 。
the second myth is , there are treatments that can help slow , reverse , or even stop aging .	第二個迷思是 , 有治療方法可以協助緩慢、逆轉 , 甚至阻止衰老 。
when you think of it , there is 99 things that can age us .	當你想一想 , 有99件事情可以讓我們老化 。
deprive your brain of oxygen for just a few minutes , those brain cells die , they never come back .	只要幾分鐘 , 腦細胞就死了 , 它們就永遠不會回來 。
play tennis too hard , on your knees , ruin your cartilage , the cartilage never comes back .	玩網球太硬 , 在你的膝蓋上 , 毀掉你的軟骨 , 軟骨永遠不會回來 。
our arteries can clog . our brains can gunk up with plaque , and we can get alzheimer's .	我們的動脈可以堵塞 , 我們的大腦可以用斑塊槍擊 , 我們可以得到阿茲海默症 。
there is just too many things to go wrong .	有太多事情要出錯 。
our bodies have 35 trillion cells , trillion with a " t . " we're talking national debt numbers here .	我們的身體有35兆個細胞 , 用一個 「 t 」 的 「 t 」 , 我們在這裡談的是國家債務 。
those cells turn themselves over once every eight years .	這些細胞每八年就轉一次 。
and every time they turn themselves over there is some damage . and that damage builds up .	每當他們轉身時 , 就會產生一些傷害 , 造成損害 。
and it builds up exponentially .	以指數的方式來建造 。
it's a little bit like the days when we all had beatles albums or eagles albums and we'd make a copy of that on a cassette tape , and let our friends copy that cassette tape , and pretty soon , with successive generations that tape sounds like garbage .	有點像日子 , 當我們有披頭四或老鷹專輯時 , 我們會在膠帶上複製 , 讓我們的朋友複製膠帶 , 很快地 , 有了成功的世代 , 聽起來像是垃圾 。
well , the same things happen to our cells .	同樣的事情也發生在我們的細胞身上 。
that's why a 65yearold person is aging at a rate of about 125 times faster than a 12yearold person .	這就是為什麼一個65歲的人老化速度比一個12歲的人快125倍
so , if there is nothing you can do to slow your aging or stop your aging , what am i doing here ?	所以 , 如果沒有什麼能讓你的老化或停止你的老化 , 我在這裡做什麼 ?
well , the fact of the matter is the best science tells us that the capacity of the human body , my body , your body , is about 90 years , a little bit more for women .	事實上 , 最好的科學告訴我們 , 人類身體的能力 , 我的身體 , 你的身體 , 大約是90年 , 女性的能力 。
but life expectancy in this country is only 78 .	但在這個國家的預期壽命只有78歲 。
so somewhere along the line , we're leaving about 12 good years on the table .	在這條線的某處 , 我們留下了大約12年的美好日子 。
these are years that we could get .	這些都是我們能得到的 。
and research shows that they would be years largely free of chronic disease , heart disease , cancer and diabetes .	研究顯示 , 大部分的疾病是慢性疾病、心臟病、癌症和糖尿病 。
we think the best way to get these missing years is to look at the cultures around the world that are actually experiencing them , areas where people are living to age 100 at rates up to 10 times greater than we are , areas where the life expectancy is an extra dozen years , the rate of middle age mortality is a fraction of what it is in this country .	我們認為最好的方法就是去看世界各地的文化 , 去體驗他們 , 在那裡 , 人們活到一百歲 , 比我們多十倍 , 預期壽命是十多年 , 中年死亡率是這個國家的一部分 。
we found our first blue zone about 125 miles off the coast of italy , on the island of sardinia .	我們發現我們在義大利海岸的第一塊藍色區域 , 位在薩丁尼亞島 。
and not the entire island , the island is about 1 . 4 million people , but only up in the highlands , an area called the nuoro province .	不是整個島嶼 , 島嶼大約有一百四十萬人 , 但只有在高地 , 一個叫做nuoro省的區域 。
and here we have this area where men live the longest , about 10 times more centenarians than we have here in america .	在這裡 , 男性生活最長的地區 , 大約是美國有10倍的青少年 。
and this is a place where people not only reach age 100 , they do so with extraordinary vigor .	這個地方 , 人們不僅到達一百歲 , 他們也和非凡的優勢相處 。
places where 102 year olds still ride their bike to work , chop wood , and can beat a guy 60 years younger than them .	那裡有102歲的老人仍然騎腳踏車去工作 , chopod , 可以打得比他們年輕60年 。
their history actually goes back to about the time of christ .	他們的歷史其實回到基督的時代 。
it's actually a bronze age culture that's been isolated .	它實際上是一個被隔離出來的青銅時代文化 。
because the land is so infertile , they largely are shepherds , which occasions regular , lowintensity physical activity .	因為土地是如此的不足 , 大部份是牧羊人 , 偶爾會是低強度的實體活動 。
their diet is mostly plantbased , accentuated with foods that they can carry into the fields .	牠們的飲食主要是植物 , 牠們的食物會被集中在田野中 。
they came up with an unleavened whole wheat bread called carta musica made out of durum wheat , a type of cheese made from grassfed animals so the cheese is high in omega3 fatty acids instead of omega6 fatty acids from cornfed animals , and a type of wine that has three times the level of polyphenols than any known wine in the world .	他們想出了一整隻獨特的麥田 , 叫卡塔•麥德 , 用草原製成的一種乳酪 , 乳酪是omega-3脂肪酸 , 而不是omega-6脂肪酸 , 而是來自玉米的動物 , 還有一種葡萄酒 , 有三倍的葡萄級 , 比世界上任何已知葡萄酒量都多三倍 。
but the real secret i think lies more in the way that they organize their society .	但我認為真正的秘密是他們組織社會的方式 。
and one of the most salient elements of the sardinian society is how they treat older people .	薩丁尼亞社會最吸引人的元素之一 , 就是他們對待老年人的方式 。
you ever notice here in america , social equity seems to peak at about age 24 ?	你有沒有注意到在美國 , 社會平等似乎在24歲時達到高峰 ?
just look at the advertisements .	看看廣告 。
here in sardinia , the older you get the more equity you have , the more wisdom you're celebrated for .	在薩丁尼亞 , 你得到越多的平等 , 你就越有智慧 。
you go into the bars in sardinia , instead of seeing the sports illustrated swimsuit calendar , you see the centenarian of the month calendar .	你去了薩丁尼亞的酒吧 , 而不是看運動會描述游泳日曆 , 你看到月曆的中亞人 。
this , as it turns out , is not only good for your aging parents to keep them close to the family it imparts about four to six years of extra life expectancy research shows it's also good for the children of those families , who have lower rates of mortality and lower rates of disease .	事實證明 , 這不只適合你的老年父母 , 讓他們和家人密切相關 , 大約四到六年的預期壽命研究顯示 , 對那些家庭的孩子來說 , 死亡率較低、較低的疾病率 。
that's called the grandmother effect .	叫做祖母效應 。
we found our second blue zone on the other side of the planet , about 800 miles south of tokyo , on the archipelago of okinawa .	我們在地球的另一端發現了第二個藍色區域 , 大約有800英哩南東東京 , 位於奧克蘭哥 。
okinawa is actually 161 small islands .	okinawa實際上是161個小島 。
and in the northern part of the main island , this is ground zero for world longevity .	在主要島嶼的北部 , 這是世界長壽的基礎 。
this is a place where the oldest living female population is found .	這是最古老的女性族群被發現的地方 。
it's a place where people have the longest disabilityfree life expectancy in the world .	這個地方 , 人們有世界上最長的殘疾預期壽命 。
they have what we want .	他們有我們想要的 。
they live a long time , and tend to die in their sleep , very quickly , and often , i can tell you , after sex .	牠們活很久 , 牠們的睡眠很快 , 通常 , 我可以告訴你 , 性行為之後 。
they live about seven good years longer than the average american .	他們的壽命比一般美國人多七年 。
five times as many centenarians as we have in america .	美國有五倍之多 。
one fifth the rate of colon and breast cancer , big killers here in america .	五分之一的殖民和乳癌 , 在美國這裡有大型殺手 。
and one sixth the rate of cardiovascular disease .	心血管疾病的機率是六分之一 。
and the fact that this culture has yielded these numbers suggests strongly they have something to teach us .	而這個文化的事實證明了這些數字他們有強烈的教導我們 。
what do they do ?	他們會怎麼做 ?
once again , a plantbased diet , full of vegetables with lots of color in them .	再一次 , 一個植物的飲食 , 裡面有許多顏色的蔬菜 。
and they eat about eight times as much tofu as americans do .	他們吃大約八倍多的豆腐 , 如美國人一樣 。
more significant than what they eat is how they eat it .	比他們吃的東西更重要的是他們如何吃它 。
they have all kinds of little strategies to keep from overeating , which , as you know , is a big problem here in america .	他們有各式各樣的策略來避免過度濫用 , 如你所知 , 在美國是個大問題 。
a few of the strategies we observed: they eat off of smaller plates , so they tend to eat fewer calories at every sitting .	我們觀察到的一些策略:它們吃掉較小的盤子 , 所以它們每一處都會吃少的卡路里 。
instead of serving family style , where you can sort of mindlessly eat as you're talking , they serve at the counter , put the food away , and then bring it to the table .	與其服務家庭風格 , 不如你在說話時 , 人們可以無心地吃東西 , 把食物放在櫃子上 , 然後把食物送到桌子上 。
they also have a 3 , 000yearold adage , which i think is the greatest sort of diet suggestion ever invented .	他們還有3000歲的老年人 , 我覺得這是史上最偉大的飲食建議 。
it was invented by confucius .	它是由混合物發明的 。
and that diet is known as the hara , hatchi , bu diet .	飲食被稱為騷擾、仇恨、飲食 。
it's simply a little saying these people say before their meal to remind them to stop eating when their stomach is [80] percent full .	這只是一個小小的說 , 在他們的餐點之前 , 提醒他們不要再吃掉他們 , 因為他們的胃是80% 。
it takes about a half hour for that full feeling to travel from your belly to your brain .	要花大約半小時才能從腹部傳到腦部 。
and by remembering to stop at 80 percent it helps keep you from doing that very thing .	藉由記住 , 阻止百分之八十的情況 , 讓你無法做到那樣的事情 。
but , like sardinia , okinawa has a few social constructs that we can associate with longevity .	但 , 如薩丁尼亞 , okinawa有幾個社會建構 , 我們能與長壽相關 。
we know that isolation kills .	我們知道隔離會致命 。
fifteen years ago , the average american had three good friends .	十五年前 , 美國人平均有三個好朋友 。
we're down to one and half right now .	我們現在只有1.5歲 。
if you were lucky enough to be born in okinawa , you were born into a system where you automatically have a half a dozen friends with whom you travel through life .	如果你很幸運 , 出生在okinawa , 你出生在一個系統中 , 你就有一半的朋友 , 和你經歷過人生 。
they call it a moai . and if you're in a moai you're expected to share the bounty if you encounter luck , and if things go bad , child gets sick , parent dies , you always have somebody who has your back .	他們稱它為moai 。 如果你在moai , 你預期如果你遇到運氣不好 , 如果事情不好 , 孩子會生病 , 父母會死 , 你總是有你的後遺 。
this particular moai , these five ladies have been together for 97 years .	這個特別的moai , 這五位女士花了九十七年的時間 。
their average age is 102 .	他們的平均年齡是102歲 。
typically in america we've divided our adult life up into two sections .	通常在美國 , 我們把我們的成年生活分為兩部分 。
there is our work life , where we're productive .	我們的工作是有生產力的 。
and then one day , boom , we retire .	然後有一天 , 我們退休了 。
and typically that has meant retiring to the easy chair , or going down to arizona to play golf .	一般來說 , 這意味著退縮到簡單的椅子上 , 或是到亞利桑那州去打高爾夫球 。
in the okinawan language there is not even a word for retirement .	在奧克丁語中 , 甚至沒有退休的詞語 。
instead there is one word that imbues your entire life , and that word is " ikigai . "	取而代之的是 , 一個詞 , 就是 「 ikigai 」 。
and , roughly translated , it means " the reason for which you wake up in the morning . "	大約翻譯的意思是 「 你早上醒來的理由 」 。
for this 102yearold karate master , his ikigai was carrying forth this martial art .	這位十二歲的凱特大師 , 他的ikigai正帶著這場遊行藝術 。
for this hundredyearold fisherman it was continuing to catch fish for his family three times a week .	在這一百歲的漁夫 , 每週捕到他的家人魚三次 。
and this is a question . the national institute on aging actually gave us a questionnaire to give these centenarians .	這是個問題 。 國家老化的研究所實際上給了我們一個問卷 , 給了這些中年人 。
and one of the questions , they were very culturally astute , the people who put the questionnaire .	其中一個問題是 , 他們在文化上是很明顯的 , 那些提出質疑的人 。
one of the questions was , " what is your ikigai ? "	其中一個問題是: 「 你的ikigai是什麼 ? 」
they instantly knew why they woke up in the morning .	他們馬上就知道為什麼他們早上醒來 。
for this 102 year old woman , her ikigai was simply her greatgreatgreatgranddaughter .	在這十二歲的老女人中 , 她的曾曾曾曾曾曾祖父 。
two girls separated in age by 101 and a half years .	兩個女孩在101歲和半年之間分離 。
and i asked her what it felt like to hold a greatgreatgreatgranddaughter .	我問她 , 拿著曾曾祖父的感覺是怎樣的感覺 。
and she put her head back and she said , " it feels like leaping into heaven . "	她把她的頭放回去 , 說: 「 感覺就像是進入天堂 。 」
i thought that was a wonderful thought .	我以為那是個很棒的思想 。
my editor at geographic wanted me to find america's blue zone .	我在地理雜誌的編輯希望我能找到美國的藍色區 。
and for a while we looked on the prairies of minnesota , where actually there is a very high proportion of centenarians .	有一陣子 , 我們在明尼蘇達的展覽上看 , 實際上 , 有非常高的比例是中尼亞人 。
but that's because all the young people left .	但那是因為所有的年輕人都離開了 。
so , we turned to the data again .	所以 , 我們再次轉向數據 。
and we found america's longestlived population among the seventhday adventists concentrated in and around loma linda , california .	我們發現美國最長壽的人口 , 在加州 , 七天的廣告家集中在加州 , 和加州的羅馬林達州 。
adventists are conservative methodists .	傳統主義者是保守主義者 。
they celebrate their sabbath from sunset on friday till sunset on saturday .	他們在星期五的星期六從日出慶祝他們的日子 。
a " 24hour sanctuary in time , " they call it .	一個 「 24小時的聖誕老人 」 , 他們稱之為 「 24小時 」 。
and they follow five little habits that conveys to them extraordinary longevity , comparatively speaking .	他們遵循五個小習慣 , 傳遞給他們非凡長壽 , 相較之下的說法 。
in america here , life expectancy for the average woman is 80 .	在美國 , 平均女性平均壽命是八十歲 。
but for an adventist woman , their life expectancy is 89 .	但對於一位傳統的女性來說 , 他們的壽命是89 。
and the difference is even more pronounced among men , who are expected to live about 11 years longer than their american counterparts .	不同之處在於 , 比起他們的美國人 , 他們預期壽命比他們的美國人壽命還要長十一歲 。
now , this is a study that followed about 70 , 000 people for 30 years .	這個研究追蹤了大約七萬人 , 三十年來 。
sterling study . and i think it supremely illustrates the premise of this blue zone project .	史特林研究 。 我認為它會很快地說明了這個藍色區域的前提 。
this is a heterogeneous community .	這是一個異常的社區 。
it's white , black , hispanic , asian .	是白人、黑人、西班牙裔、亞洲人 。
the only thing that they have in common are a set of very small lifestyle habits that they follow ritualistically for most of their lives .	他們唯一共通點 , 是一組非常小的生活習慣 , 以至於他們生活中大部分的習慣 。
they take their diet directly from the bible .	他們直接從聖經中直接吃掉他們的飲食 。
genesis: chapter one , verse [29] , where god talks about legumes and seeds , and on one more stanza about green plants , ostensibly missing is meat .	第一章 , 一章 , 一章 , 上帝談到 「 肢體和種子 」 , 另一種是關於綠色植物的斯坦尚 , 最好是缺少肉 。
they take this sanctuary in time very serious .	他們認真看待這個聖誕老人 。
for 24 hours every week , no matter how busy they are , how stressed out they are at work , where the kids need to be driven , they stop everything and they focus on their god , their social network , and then , hardwired right in the religion , are nature walks .	每週24小時 , 不管他們有多忙 , 他們在工作上有多壓力 , 孩子需要被驅動 , 他們會停止一切 , 他們會把焦點放在他們的上帝、他們的社交網路 , 接著 , 在宗教中 , 硬線是自然的走路 。
and the power of this is not that it's done occasionally , the power is it's done every week for a lifetime .	這項技術的力量並不是偶爾完成的 , 權力是每週都在完成的 。
none of it's hard . none of it costs money .	沒有錢 , 沒有錢 。
adventists also tend to hang out with other adventists .	傳統主義者也傾向和其他的冒險家結合 。
so , if you go to an adventist's party you don't see people swilling jim beam or rolling a joint .	所以 , 若你去參加一位傳統主義者的派對 , 你不會看到人們在流汗或滾動一個關節 。
instead they're talking about their next nature walk , exchanging recipes , and yes , they pray .	相反地 , 他們在談論他們的下一步 , 交換食譜 , 是的 , 他們祈禱 。
but they influence each other in profound and measurable ways .	但它們會以深刻且可測量的方式影響彼此 。
this is a culture that has yielded ellsworth whareham .	這是一種文化 , 這種文化已經產出了不少美麗的沃爾蒙 。
ellsworth whareham is 97 years old .	埃爾斯威爾•沃爾罕是97歲 。
he's a multimillionaire , yet when a contractor wanted 6 , 000 dollars to build a privacy fence , he said , " for that kind of money i'll do it myself . "	他是多百萬富翁 , 但當一個承包商想要建造一個隱私的柵欄時 , 他說: 「 為了我自己所付出的錢 。 」
so for the next three days he was out shoveling cement , and hauling poles around .	所以接下來的三天 , 他在外面的水泥 , 拖著兩極 。
and predictably , perhaps , on the fourth day he ended up in the operating room .	可以預測 , 也許 , 在他在手術室的第四天 , 他終於在手術室裡 。
but not as the guy on the table ; the guy doing openheart surgery .	但不是桌上的那個人 , 而是開心手術的那個人 。
at 97 he still does 20 openheart surgeries every month .	九十七歲時 , 他每個月都會進行二十次開心手術 。
ed rawlings , 103 years old now , an active cowboy , starts his morning with a swim .	愛德華•魯林斯 , 103歲 , 一個活躍的牛仔 , 早上開始游泳 。
and on weekends he likes to put on the boards , throw up rooster tails .	週末 , 他喜歡在董事會上 , 扔掉屋頂的尾巴 。
her grandson actually lives in the twin cities here .	她的孫子其實住在這兒 。
she starts her day with lifting weights .	她每天從升起的重量開始 。
she rides her bicycle .	她騎腳踏車 。
and then she gets in her rootbeer colored 1994 cadillac seville , and tears down the san bernardino freeway , where she still volunteers for seven different organizations .	然後她走進她的根部 , 穿著1994年的卡迪拉•塞維爾 , 穿著聖柏納多的高速公路 , 在那裡 , 她仍然自願參加七個不同的組織 。
i've been on 19 hardcore expeditions .	我曾參加過19個硬幣的探險 。
i'm probably the only person you'll ever meet who rode his bicycle across the sahara desert without sunscreen .	我可能是你唯一能見的人 , 穿越撒哈拉沙漠的腳踏車 , 穿越撒哈拉沙漠 。
but i'll tell you , there is no adventure more harrowing than riding shotgun with marge deton .	但我要告訴各位 , 沒有任何冒險 , 比騎馬•德頓的攝影機更有傷害 。
" a stranger is a friend i haven't met yet ! " she'd say to me .	「 我還沒見過一個陌生人 ! 」 她對我說:
so , what are the common denominators in these three cultures ?	所以 , 這三種文化中有什麼共同點 ?
what are the things that they all do ?	他們所有人都在做什麼 ?
and we managed to boil it down to nine .	我們成功地將它歸結為九個 。
in fact we've done two more blue zone expeditions since this and these common denominators hold true .	事實上 , 自此以來 , 我們已經做了兩個藍色的探險 , 這些共同的決策者持有真相 。
and the first one , and i'm about to utter a heresy here , none of them exercise , at least the way we think of exercise .	首先 , 我將要給你們一個玩具 , 沒有一個練習 , 至少我們對運動的看法 。
instead , they set up their lives so that they are constantly nudged into physical activity .	相反地 , 他們設立了自己的生命 , 這樣他們就不斷地被推動到實體活動中 。
these 100yearold okinawan women are getting up and down off the ground , they sit on the floor , 30 or 40 times a day .	這一百歲的俄亥俄州的婦女正在上地下 , 他們每天都坐在地板上 , 30或40次 。
sardinians live in vertical houses , up and down the stairs .	薩丁尼亞人住在垂直的房子 , 上下樓梯 。
every trip to the store , or to church or to a friend's house occasions a walk .	每次旅行到商店、教堂或朋友家 , 都偶爾會走路 。
they don't have any conveniences .	他們沒有任何方便 。
there is not a button to push to do yard work or house work .	沒有一個按鈕 , 去做院子工作或房子工作 。
